Django Example 2: Multi-Tenant Stream Groups 
# services/tenant_stream_setup.py
import redis
from django.db import models
from .models import Author

redis_client = redis.Redis(host='localhost', port=6379, decode_responses=True)

class StreamGroupManager:
    @staticmethod
    def setup_company_groups():
        """Create consumer groups for each company"""
        
        companies = Author.objects.values_list('company', flat=True).distinct()
        
        for company in companies:
            company_key = company.replace(' ', '_').lower()
            
            try:
                # Create company-specific application processing group
                redis_client.xgroup_create(
                    f'company_applications:{company_key}',
                    f'{company_key}_hr_team',
                    '$',
                    mkstream=True
                )
                print(f"✅ Created HR group for {company}")
                
                # Create company-specific analytics group
                redis_client.xgroup_create(
                    f'company_applications:{company_key}',
                    f'{company_key}_analytics', 
                    '0',  # Process all historical data
                    mkstream=True
                )
                print(f"📊 Created analytics group for {company}")
                
                # Create company notification group
                redis_client.xgroup_create(
                    'notifications:job_posts',
                    f'{company_key}_notifications',
                    '$',
                    mkstream=True
                )
                print(f"🔔 Created notifications group for {company}")
                
            except Exception as e:
                if "BUSYGROUP" not in str(e):
                    print(f"❌ Error creating groups for {company}: {e}")
    
    @staticmethod
    def setup_skill_based_groups():
        """Create consumer groups for skill-based job matching"""
        
        from .models import Skills
        skills = Skills.objects.all()
        
        for skill in skills:
            skill_key = skill.name.lower().replace(' ', '_')
            
            try:
                # Create skill-specific processing group
                redis_client.xgroup_create(
                    f'notifications:skill:{skill_key}',
                    f'skill_matcher_{skill_key}',
                    '$',
                    mkstream=True
                )
                print(f"🎯 Created skill group for {skill.name}")
                
                # Create skill analytics group  
                redis_client.xgroup_create(
                    f'notifications:skill:{skill_key}',
                    f'skill_analytics_{skill_key}',
                    '0',
                    mkstream=True
                )
                print(f"📈 Created skill analytics for {skill.name}")
                
            except Exception as e:
                if "BUSYGROUP" not in str(e):
                    print(f"❌ Error for skill {skill.name}: {e}")

XREADGROUP - Read from Consumer Group

Purpose: Read entries from a stream as part of a consumer group, providing load balancing and message delivery guarantees.
Syntax: XREADGROUP GROUP group consumer [COUNT count] [BLOCK milliseconds] [NOACK] STREAMS key [key ...] ID [ID ...]
Parameters:
  • GROUP group consumer - Consumer group and consumer name
  • COUNT - Maximum number of entries
  • BLOCK - Block waiting for entries
  • NOACK - Don't add to pending entries list
  • > - Read new entries not delivered to group

Return: Array of streams with entries assigned to this consumer
Django Example 1: Application Processing Worker 
# management/commands/process_applications.py
import redis
import time
import json
from django.core.management.base import BaseCommand
from django.core.mail import send_mail
from .models import JobPost, User

redis_client = redis.Redis(host='localhost', port=6379, decode_responses=True)

class Command(BaseCommand):
    help = 'Process job applications from stream'
    
    def add_arguments(self, parser):
        parser.add_argument('--consumer-name', default='worker-1', help='Consumer name')
        parser.add_argument('--batch-size', type=int, default=5, help='Batch size')
    
    def handle(self, *args, **options):
        consumer_name = options['consumer_name']
        batch_size = options['batch_size']
        
        self.stdout.write(f"🚀 Starting application processor: {consumer_name}")
        
        while True:
            try:
                # Read from application processing group
                result = redis_client.xreadgroup(
                    'application_processors',  # group name
                    consumer_name,             # consumer name
                    streams={'job_applications': '>'},  # '>' means new entries
                    count=batch_size,
                    block=30000  # Block for 30 seconds
                )
                
                if result:
                    for stream_name, entries in result:
                        self.process_application_batch(entries, consumer_name)
                else:
                    self.stdout.write("⏰ No new applications - waiting...")
                    
            except KeyboardInterrupt:
                self.stdout.write("❌ Worker stopped")
                break
            except Exception as e:
                self.stdout.write(f"⚠️ Processing error: {e}")
                time.sleep(5)
    
    def process_application_batch(self, entries, consumer_name):
        self.stdout.write(f"📦 Processing batch of {len(entries)} applications...")
        
        for entry_id, fields in entries:
            try:
                # Process individual application
                job_id = fields.get('job_id')
                applicant_email = fields.get('applicant_email')
                
                self.stdout.write(
                    f"  🔍 Processing [{entry_id}]\n"
                    f"     Job: {fields.get('job_title')}\n"
                    f"     Applicant: {applicant_email}\n"
                    f"     Company: {fields.get('company')}\n"
                    f"     Consumer: {consumer_name}"
                )
                
                # Simulate processing steps
                self.validate_application(fields)
                self.score_application(fields)
                self.send_confirmation_email(fields)
                
                # Acknowledge successful processing
                redis_client.xack('job_applications', 'application_processors', entry_id)
                self.stdout.write(f"  ✅ Completed [{entry_id}]")
                
            except Exception as e:
                self.stdout.write(f"  ❌ Failed [{entry_id}]: {e}")
                # Leave in pending list for retry
    
    def validate_application(self, fields):
        # Application validation logic
        required_fields = ['job_id', 'applicant_email', 'job_title']
        for field in required_fields:
            if not fields.get(field):
                raise ValueError(f"Missing required field: {field}")
    
    def score_application(self, fields):
        # Simple scoring based on salary expectations
        salary = int(fields.get('salary', 0))
        score = min(salary // 1000, 100)  # Score out of 100
        return score
    
    def send_confirmation_email(self, fields):
        # Send confirmation email to applicant
        subject = f"Application Received: {fields.get('job_title')}"
        message = f"""
        Dear Applicant,
        
        We've received your application for {fields.get('job_title')} at {fields.get('company')}.
        
        Application details:
        - Position: {fields.get('job_title')}
        - Company: {fields.get('company')}  
        - Location: {fields.get('location')}
        - Salary: ${fields.get('salary')}
        
        We'll review your application and get back to you soon.
        
        Best regards,
        HR Team
        """
        
        # Simulate email sending
        self.stdout.write(f"  📧 Confirmation email sent to {fields.get('applicant_email')}")
Printout:

Django Example 2: Analytics Processing Worker 
# management/commands/analytics_processor.py
import redis
from django.core.management.base import BaseCommand
from django.utils import timezone
from collections import defaultdict, Counter
import json

redis_client = redis.Redis(host='localhost', port=6379, decode_responses=True)

class Command(BaseCommand):
    help = 'Process applications for analytics and insights'
    
    def handle(self, *args, **options):
        consumer_name = f"analytics-worker-{timezone.now().strftime('%H%M%S')}"
        
        self.stdout.write(f"📊 Starting analytics processor: {consumer_name}")
        
        # Analytics data structures
        daily_stats = defaultdict(int)
        company_stats = defaultdict(int)
        skill_demand = Counter()
        salary_ranges = []
        
        while True:
            try:
                result = redis_client.xreadgroup(
                    'analytics_team',
                    consumer_name,
                    streams={'job_applications': '>'},
                    count=10,
                    block=15000
                )
                
                if result:
                    for stream_name, entries in result:
                        for entry_id, fields in entries:
                            self.process_for_analytics(
                                entry_id, fields, daily_stats, 
                                company_stats, skill_demand, salary_ranges
                            )
                            
                    # Generate periodic reports
                    self.generate_analytics_report(
                        daily_stats, company_stats, skill_demand, salary_ranges
                    )
                        
            except KeyboardInterrupt:
                self.stdout.write("📈 Analytics processor stopped")
                break
            except Exception as e:
                self.stdout.write(f"⚠️ Analytics error: {e}")
    
    def process_for_analytics(self, entry_id, fields, daily_stats, 
                            company_stats, skill_demand, salary_ranges):
        try:
            # Extract analytics data
            company = fields.get('company', 'unknown')
            salary = int(fields.get('salary', 0))
            timestamp = fields.get('timestamp', '')
            date = timestamp.split('T')[0] if timestamp else 'unknown'
            
            # Update statistics
            daily_stats[date] += 1
            company_stats[company] += 1
            salary_ranges.append(salary)
            
            # Track skills demand (if available in application)
            if 'skills' in fields:
                skills = fields['skills'].split(',')
                for skill in skills:
                    skill_demand[skill.strip()] += 1
            
            # Store processed analytics entry
            redis_client.xadd(
                'analytics_processed',
                {
                    'original_entry_id': entry_id,
                    'company': company,
                    'salary': str(salary),
                    'date': date,
                    'processing_time': timezone.now().isoformat(),
                    'processor': 'analytics_team'
                }
            )
            
            # Acknowledge processing
            redis_client.xack('job_applications', 'analytics_team', entry_id)
            
            self.stdout.write(f"📈 Analyzed [{entry_id}] - {company}: ${salary}")
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.stdout.write(f"❌ Analytics error for [{entry_id}]: {e}")
    
    def generate_analytics_report(self, daily_stats, company_stats, 
                                skill_demand, salary_ranges):
        if not salary_ranges:
            return
            
        # Calculate salary statistics
        avg_salary = sum(salary_ranges) / len(salary_ranges)
        min_salary = min(salary_ranges)
        max_salary = max(salary_ranges)
        
        report = {
            'timestamp': timezone.now().isoformat(),
            'total_applications': len(salary_ranges),
            'salary_stats': {
                'average': f"${avg_salary:,.2f}",
                'min': f"${min_salary:,}",
                'max': f"${max_salary:,}"
            },
            'top_companies': dict(company_stats.most_common(5)),
            'daily_breakdown': dict(daily_stats),
            'skill_demand': dict(skill_demand.most_common(10))
        }
        
        # Store report in Redis
        redis_client.set(
            f'analytics_report:{timezone.now().date()}',
            json.dumps(report),
            ex=86400  # Expire after 1 day
        )
        
        self.stdout.write(
            f"\n📊 ANALYTICS REPORT\n"
            f"   Total Applications: {report['total_applications']}\n"
            f"   Average Salary: {report['salary_stats']['average']}\n"
            f"   Top Company: {list(company_stats.keys())[0] if company_stats else 'N/A'}\n"
            f"   Most Demanded Skill: {skill_demand.most_common(1)[0][0] if skill_demand else 'N/A'}\n"
        )
Printout:

📈 Analyzed [1693920011000-0] - ABC Corp: $80000
📈 Analyzed [1693920011001-0] - XYZ Inc: $75000

XACK - Acknowledge Entry Processing

Purpose: Acknowledge that entries have been successfully processed by a consumer, removing them from the pending list.
Syntax: XACK key group ID [ID ...]
Parameters:
  • key - Stream name
  • group - Consumer group name
  • ID - Entry ID(s) to acknowledge

Return: Number of entries acknowledged
Django Example 1: Reliable Email Processing 
# services/email_processor.py
import redis
from django.core.mail import send_mail
from django.template.loader import render_to_string
from django.conf import settings
import logging

redis_client = redis.Redis(host='localhost', port=6379, decode_responses=True)
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class EmailProcessorService:
    def __init__(self, consumer_name='email-processor'):
        self.consumer_name = consumer_name
        self.group_name = 'email_notifications'
        self.stream_name = 'job_applications'
    
    def process_email_queue(self):
        """Process emails with reliable acknowledgment"""
        
        while True:
            try:
                # Read pending emails first (failed previous attempts)
                pending_result = redis_client.xreadgroup(
                    self.group_name,
                    self.consumer_name,
                    streams={self.stream_name: '0'},  # '0' gets pending entries
                    count=5
                )
                
                if pending_result:
                    logger.info(f"🔄 Processing {len(pending_result[0][1])} pending emails")
                    self.process_email_batch(pending_result[0][1], is_retry=True)
                
                # Read new entries
                new_result = redis_client.xreadgroup(
                    self.group_name, 
                    self.consumer_name,
                    streams={self.stream_name: '>'},  # '>' gets new entries
                    count=10,
                    block=20000
                )
                
                if new_result:
                    logger.info(f"📧 Processing {len(new_result[0][1])} new emails")
                    self.process_email_batch(new_result[0][1], is_retry=False)
                    
            except KeyboardInterrupt:
                logger.info("📧 Email processor stopped")
                break
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"⚠️ Email processing error: {e}")
    
    def process_email_batch(self, entries, is_retry=False):
        """Process batch of email entries with proper acknowledgment"""
        
        for entry_id, fields in entries:
            try:
                # Extract email details
                recipient_email = fields.get('applicant_email')
                job_title = fields.get('job_title')
                company = fields.get('company')
                applicant_name = fields.get('applicant_name', 'Applicant')
                
                if not recipient_email or not job_title:
                    logger.warning(f"⚠️ Missing email data in [{entry_id}]")
                    continue
                
                # Send confirmation email
                success = self.send_application_confirmation(
                    recipient_email, job_title, company, applicant_name, is_retry
                )
                
                if success:
                    # Acknowledge successful email sending
                    ack_result = redis_client.xack(
                        self.stream_name, 
                        self.group_name, 
                        entry_id
                    )
                    
                    if ack_result:
                        logger.info(f"✅ Email sent and acknowledged [{entry_id}]")
                        
                        # Store successful email log
                        redis_client.xadd(
                            'email_sent_log',
                            {
                                'original_entry_id': entry_id,
                                'recipient': recipient_email,
                                'job_title': job_title,
                                'company': company,
                                'retry_attempt': 'yes' if is_retry else 'no',
                                'sent_at': timezone.now().isoformat(),
                                'processor': self.consumer_name
                            }
                        )
                    else:
                        logger.error(f"❌ Failed to acknowledge [{entry_id}]")
                else:
                    logger.error(f"📧 Email sending failed for [{entry_id}] - left in pending")
                    
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"❌ Email processing error [{entry_id}]: {e}")
                # Don't acknowledge on error - entry stays in pending list
    
    def send_application_confirmation(self, recipient_email, job_title, 
                                    company, applicant_name, is_retry):
        """Send application confirmation email"""
        try:
            subject = f"Application Received: {job_title} at {company}"
            
            # Use Django template for professional email
            email_context = {
                'applicant_name': applicant_name,
                'job_title': job_title,
                'company': company,
                'application_date': timezone.now().date(),
                'is_retry': is_retry
            }
            
            html_message = render_to_string(
                'emails/application_confirmation.html', 
                email_context
            )
            plain_message = render_to_string(
                'emails/application_confirmation.txt',
                email_context  
            )
            
            send_mail(
                subject=subject,
                message=plain_message,
                from_email=settings.DEFAULT_FROM_EMAIL,
                recipient_list=[recipient_email],
                html_message=html_message,
                fail_silently=False
            )
            
            retry_note = " (RETRY)" if is_retry else ""
            logger.info(f"📧 Email sent to {recipient_email}{retry_note}")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"📧 Email sending failed to {recipient_email}: {e}")
            return False
Printout: 
🔄 Processing 2 pending emails
📧 Email sent to jane.smith@example.com (RETRY)
✅ Email sent and acknowledged [1693920012000-0]
📧 Email sent to mike.johnson@example.com (RETRY)  
✅ Email sent and acknowledged [1693920012001-0]

📧 Processing 3 new emails
📧 Email sent to sarah.davis@example.com
✅ Email sent and acknowledged [1693920013000-0]
📧 Email sent to david.wilson@example.com

- Failed emails: 0
Django Example 2: Priority Processing with Acknowledgment 
# management/commands/priority_processor.py
import redis
from django.core.management.base import BaseCommand
from django.core.mail import send_mail
from django.contrib.auth.models import User
from django.utils import timezone
from .models import JobPost, Author

redis_client = redis.Redis(host='localhost', port=6379, decode_responses=True)

class Command(BaseCommand):
    help = 'Process high-priority applications (high salary/urgent)'
    
    def handle(self, *args, **options):
        consumer_name = 'priority-processor-1'
        group_name = 'priority_processing'
        
        self.stdout.write(f"⚡ Starting priority processor: {consumer_name}")
        
        processed_count = 0
        acknowledged_count = 0
        
        while True:
            try:
                result = redis_client.xreadgroup(
                    group_name,
                    consumer_name,
                    streams={'job_applications': '>'},
                    count=3,  # Small batches for priority processing
                    block=10000
                )
                
                if result:
                    for stream_name, entries in result:
                        for entry_id, fields in entries:
                            processed_count += 1
                            
                            if self.is_priority_application(fields):
                                success = self.process_priority_application(entry_id, fields)
                                
                                if success:
                                    # Acknowledge only after successful processing
                                    ack_count = redis_client.xack(
                                        'job_applications',
                                        group_name,
                                        entry_id
                                    )
                                    
                                    if ack_count > 0:
                                        acknowledged_count += 1
                                        self.stdout.write(
                                            f"⚡ Priority application processed [{entry_id}] "
                                            f"({acknowledged_count}/{processed_count})"
                                        )
                                    else:
                                        self.stdout.write(f"⚠️ Ack failed for [{entry_id}]")
                                else:
                                    self.stdout.write(f"❌ Processing failed [{entry_id}] - not acknowledged")
                            else:
                                # Not priority - acknowledge without special processing  
                                redis_client.xack('job_applications', group_name, entry_id)
                                acknowledged_count += 1
                                
            except KeyboardInterrupt:
                self.stdout.write(
                    f"⚡ Priority processor stopped\n"
                    f"   Processed: {processed_count}\n" 
                    f"   Acknowledged: {acknowledged_count}"
                )
                break
            except Exception as e:
                self.stdout.write(f"⚠️ Priority processing error: {e}")
    
    def is_priority_application(self, fields):
        """Determine if application requires priority processing"""
        try:
            salary = int(fields.get('salary', 0))
            company = fields.get('company', '').lower()
            
            # Priority criteria
            high_salary = salary >= 85000
            premium_company = any(keyword in company for keyword in ['tech', 'google', 'microsoft', 'amazon'])
            urgent_keywords = any(keyword in fields.get('job_title', '').lower() 
                                for keyword in ['senior', 'lead', 'principal', 'director'])
            
            return high_salary or premium_company or urgent_keywords
            
        except ValueError:
            return False
    
    def process_priority_application(self, entry_id, fields):
        """Process priority applications with special handling"""
        try:
            job_title = fields.get('job_title')
            company = fields.get('company')  
            applicant_email = fields.get('applicant_email')
            salary = fields.get('salary')
            
            self.stdout.write(
                f"🎯 PRIORITY APPLICATION [{entry_id}]\n"
                f"   Job: {job_title}\n"
                f"   Company: {company}\n" 
                f"   Salary: ${salary}\n"
                f"   Applicant: {applicant_email}"
            )
            
            # 1. Send immediate notification to hiring manager
            self.notify_hiring_manager(fields)
            
            # 2. Flag in database for expedited review
            self.flag_for_expedited_review(fields)
            
            # 3. Add to priority processing log
            redis_client.xadd(
                'priority_applications_log',
                {
                    'original_entry_id': entry_id,
                    'job_title': job_title,
                    'company': company,
                    'salary': salary,
                    'applicant_email': applicant_email,
                    'priority_reason': self.get_priority_reason(fields),
                    'processed_at': timezone.now().isoformat(),
                    'processor': 'priority-processor-1',
                    'status': 'completed'
                }
            )
            
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.stdout.write(f"❌ Priority processing failed: {e}")
            return False
    
    def notify_hiring_manager(self, fields):
        """Send immediate notification to hiring manager"""
        subject = f"🚨 Priority Application: {fields.get('job_title')}"
        message = f"""
        Priority application received requiring immediate attention:
        
        Position: {fields.get('job_title')}
        Company: {fields.get('company')}
        Salary: ${fields.get('salary')}
        Applicant: {fields.get('applicant_email')}
        Location: {fields.get('location')}
        
        Please review this application as soon as possible.
        """
        
        # Send to hiring manager email
        hiring_manager_email = f"hiring@{fields.get('company', 'company').lower().replace(' ', '')}.com"
        
        self.stdout.write(f"📧 Priority notification sent to {hiring_manager_email}")
    
    def flag_for_expedited_review(self, fields):
        """Flag application in database for expedited processing"""
        self.stdout.write("🚩 Application flagged for expedited review")
    
    def get_priority_reason(self, fields):
        """Get reason why application was marked as priority"""
        reasons = []
        
        try:
            salary = int(fields.get('salary', 0))
            if salary >= 85000:
                reasons.append(f"high_salary_${salary}")
        except ValueError:
            pass
            
        company = fields.get('company', '').lower()
        if any(keyword in company for keyword in ['tech', 'google', 'microsoft', 'amazon']):
            reasons.append("premium_company")
            
        job_title = fields.get('job_title', '').lower()
        if any(keyword in job_title for keyword in ['senior', 'lead', 'principal', 'director']):
            reasons.append("senior_position")
        
        return ','.join(reasons) if reasons else 'unknown'
Printout:

XLEN - Get Stream Length

Purpose: Returns the number of entries in a stream.
Syntax: XLEN key
Parameters:
  • key - Stream name

Return: Number of entries in the stream
Django Example: Stream Monitoring Dashboard 
# views.py - Stream monitoring dashboard
import redis
from django.shortcuts import render
from django.http import JsonResponse
from django.utils import timezone

redis_client = redis.Redis(host='localhost', port=6379, decode_responses=True)

def stream_dashboard(request):
    """Dashboard showing stream statistics and health"""
    
    # Get lengths of all monitored streams
    stream_stats = {}
    
    streams_to_monitor = [
        'job_applications',
        'user_activity:1',
        'performance_metrics', 
        'notifications:job_posts',
        'email_sent_log',
        'priority_applications_log',
        'analytics_processed'
    ]
    
    for stream_name in streams_to_monitor:
        try:
            length = redis_client.xlen(stream_name)
            stream_stats[stream_name] = {
                'length': length,
                'status': 'healthy' if length < 10000 else 'warning' if length < 50000 else 'critical'
            }
        except Exception as e:
            stream_stats[stream_name] = {
                'length': 0,
                'status': 'error',
                'error': str(e)
            }
    
    # Calculate totals and health
    total_entries = sum(stats['length'] for stats in stream_stats.values() if 'error' not in stats)
    healthy_streams = sum(1 for stats in stream_stats.values() if stats.get('status') == 'healthy')
    total_streams = len(stream_stats)
    
    dashboard_data = {
        'timestamp': timezone.now().isoformat(),
        'streams': stream_stats,
        'summary': {
            'total_entries': total_entries,
            'healthy_streams': healthy_streams,
            'total_streams': total_streams,
            'health_percentage': round((healthy_streams / total_streams) * 100, 1) if total_streams > 0 else 0
        }
    }
    
    if request.headers.get('Accept') == 'application/json':
        return JsonResponse(dashboard_data)
    
    return render(request, 'dashboard/streams.html', {
        'dashboard_data': dashboard_data
    })

💡 Implementation Note: The remaining Stream commands (XDEL, XTRIM, XRANGE, XREVRANGE, XPENDING, XCLAIM, XAUTOCLAIM, XINFO, etc.) provide comprehensive tools for stream lifecycle management, data cleanup, range queries, pending entry recovery, and stream introspection in Django production environments.

🔮 Auto-suggest Commands

Redis Auto-suggest commands provide fast, intelligent autocomplete functionality using RediSearch suggestion dictionaries. Perfect for Django applications requiring search suggestions, type-ahead functionality, and smart user interfaces with contextual recommendations.

FT.SUGADD - Add Suggestion to Auto-Complete Dictionary

Purpose: Adds a suggestion string to an auto-complete suggestion dictionary for fast prefix-based search suggestions.
Syntax: FT.SUGADD key string score [INCR] [PAYLOAD payload]
Parameters:
  • key - Auto-complete dictionary name
  • string - Suggestion text to add
  • score - Suggestion weight/score for ranking
  • INCR - Increment score if suggestion exists
  • PAYLOAD - Optional metadata for the suggestion

Return: Current size of the suggestion dictionary
Django Example 1: Job Title Auto-Complete 
# management/commands/build_job_suggestions.py
import redis
from django.core.management.base import BaseCommand
from .models import JobPost

redis_client = redis.Redis(host='localhost', port=6379, decode_responses=True)

class Command(BaseCommand):
    help = 'Build job title auto-complete suggestions'
    
    def handle(self, *args, **options):
        # Get job titles with frequency counts
        job_titles = JobPost.objects.values_list('title', flat=True)
        title_counts = {}
        
        for title in job_titles:
            title_counts[title] = title_counts.get(title, 0) + 1
        
        self.stdout.write("Building job title suggestions...")
        
        # Add each title to auto-complete with frequency as score
        for title, count in title_counts.items():
            result = redis_client.execute_command(
                'FT.SUGADD', 
                'job_titles:suggestions',
                title,
                count * 10,  # Boost score for better ranking
                'PAYLOAD', f'{{"frequency": {count}, "type": "job_title"}}'
            )
            
            self.stdout.write(f"Added: {title} (score: {count * 10}) - Dict size: {result}")
        
        # Add popular variations and synonyms
        popular_titles = {
            'Software Engineer': 100,
            'Software Developer': 95, 
            'Full Stack Engineer': 90,
            'Full Stack Developer': 88,
            'Backend Engineer': 85,
            'Backend Developer': 83,
            'Frontend Engineer': 80,
            'Frontend Developer': 78,
            'DevOps Engineer': 75,
            'Data Engineer': 73,
            'Python Developer': 70,
            'JavaScript Developer': 68,
            'React Developer': 65,
            'Node.js Developer': 63
        }
        
        for title, score in popular_titles.items():
            redis_client.execute_command(
                'FT.SUGADD',
                'job_titles:suggestions', 
                title,
                score,
                'INCR',  # Increment if exists
                'PAYLOAD', f'{{"frequency": {score}, "type": "popular_title"}}'
            )
        
        total_suggestions = redis_client.execute_command('FT.SUGLEN', 'job_titles:suggestions')
        self.stdout.write(f"✅ Total suggestions in dictionary: {total_suggestions}")
Printout:

Added: Full Stack Developer (score: 120) - Dict size: 2  
Added: Data Scientist (score: 80) - Dict size: 3
Added: Frontend Developer (score: 100) - Dict size: 4

Django Example 2: Company Auto-Complete with Metadata 
# services/company_suggestions.py
import redis
from django.db.models import Count
from .models import Author, JobPost

redis_client = redis.Redis(host='localhost', port=6379, decode_responses=True)

class CompanySuggestionService:
    @staticmethod
    def build_company_suggestions():
        """Build company suggestions with hiring activity data"""
        
        # Get companies with their job posting counts
        companies = Author.objects.annotate(
            job_count=Count('jobpost'),
            active_jobs=Count('jobpost__expiry')
        ).values('company', 'job_count', 'active_jobs')
        
        print("Building company suggestions...")
        
        for company_data in companies:
            company = company_data['company']
            job_count = company_data['job_count']
            
            # Score based on hiring activity
            base_score = job_count * 15
            activity_bonus = min(company_data['active_jobs'] * 5, 50)
            final_score = base_score + activity_bonus
            
            # Rich payload with company insights
            payload = {
                'company_name': company,
                'total_jobs_posted': job_count,
                'active_jobs': company_data['active_jobs'],
                'hiring_status': 'active' if company_data['active_jobs'] > 0 else 'inactive',
                'company_size': 'enterprise' if job_count > 10 else 'startup' if job_count > 3 else 'small',
                'popularity_tier': 'high' if final_score > 100 else 'medium' if final_score > 50 else 'standard'
            }
            
            result = redis_client.execute_command(
                'FT.SUGADD',
                'companies:suggestions',
                company,
                final_score,
                'PAYLOAD', str(payload).replace("'", '"')
            )
            
            print(f"Added: {company} (score: {final_score}) - {payload['hiring_status']} - Dict size: {result}")
            
            # Add company abbreviations
            if 'Corporation' in company:
                abbrev = company.replace('Corporation', 'Corp')
                redis_client.execute_command(
                    'FT.SUGADD', 'companies:suggestions', abbrev, final_score - 10,
                    'PAYLOAD', str({**payload, 'original_name': company, 'type': 'abbreviation'}).replace("'", '"')
                )
                
        # Add well-known tech companies for reference
        tech_giants = [
            ('Google', 200, 'big_tech'), ('Apple', 195, 'big_tech'), ('Microsoft', 190, 'big_tech'),
            ('Amazon', 185, 'big_tech'), ('Meta', 180, 'big_tech'), ('Netflix', 175, 'big_tech'),
            ('Tesla', 170, 'innovative'), ('OpenAI', 165, 'ai_startup'), ('Stripe', 160, 'fintech')
        ]
        
        for company, score, category in tech_giants:
            payload = {
                'company_name': company,
                'type': 'reference_company',
                'category': category,
                'tier': 'premium',
                'global_recognition': True
            }
            
            redis_client.execute_command(
                'FT.SUGADD', 'companies:suggestions', company, score,
                'PAYLOAD', str(payload).replace("'", '"')
            )
            print(f"Added reference: {company} ({category}) - score: {score}")
    
    @staticmethod
    def get_suggestions_stats():
        total = redis_client.execute_command('FT.SUGLEN', 'companies:suggestions')
        return {'total_companies': total, 'status': 'active' if total > 0 else 'empty'}

FT.SUGGET - Get Auto-Complete Suggestions

Purpose: Retrieves completion suggestions for a prefix from an auto-complete dictionary.
Syntax: FT.SUGGET key prefix [FUZZY] [MAX num] [WITHSCORES] [WITHPAYLOADS]
Parameters:
  • key - Auto-complete dictionary name
  • prefix - Text prefix to search for
  • FUZZY - Enable fuzzy matching (typos)
  • MAX num - Maximum suggestions to return
  • WITHSCORES - Include suggestion scores
  • WITHPAYLOADS - Include suggestion payloads

Return: Array of matching suggestions with optional scores and payloads
Django Example 1: Smart Job Search API 
# views.py - Auto-complete API with smart suggestions
import redis
from django.http import JsonResponse
from django.views.decorators.csrf import csrf_exempt
import json

redis_client = redis.Redis(host='localhost', port=6379, decode_responses=True)

@csrf_exempt
def smart_autocomplete_api(request):
    """Intelligent auto-complete API with contextual suggestions"""
    
    query = request.GET.get('q', '').strip()
    category = request.GET.get('category', 'all')  # jobs, companies, skills
    max_results = int(request.GET.get('max', 8))
    user_context = request.GET.get('context', 'general')  # job_search, skill_discovery
    
    if len(query) < 2:
        return JsonResponse({'suggestions': [], 'query': query, 'count': 0})
    
    all_suggestions = []
    
    try:
        # Get job suggestions
        if category in ['all', 'jobs']:
            job_suggestions = redis_client.execute_command(
                'FT.SUGGET', 'job_titles:suggestions', query,
                'FUZZY', 'MAX', max_results, 'WITHSCORES', 'WITHPAYLOADS'
            )
            
            # Parse job suggestions (Redis returns: [text, score, payload, ...])
            for i in range(0, len(job_suggestions), 3):
                if i + 2 < len(job_suggestions):
                    text = job_suggestions[i]
                    score = float(job_suggestions[i + 1])
                    payload = json.loads(job_suggestions[i + 2]) if job_suggestions[i + 2] else {}
                    
                    # Apply contextual boosting
                    contextual_score = score
                    if user_context == 'job_search':
                        contextual_score += 20
                    if payload.get('type') == 'popular_title':
                        contextual_score += 15
                        
                    all_suggestions.append({
                        'text': text,
                        'category': 'job',
                        'score': round(contextual_score, 1),
                        'type': payload.get('type', 'job_title'),
                        'frequency': payload.get('frequency', 0),
                        'icon': '💼',
                        'boost_reason': 'Popular job title' if payload.get('type') == 'popular_title' else None
                    })
        
        # Get company suggestions  
        if category in ['all', 'companies']:
            company_suggestions = redis_client.execute_command(
                'FT.SUGGET', 'companies:suggestions', query,
                'FUZZY', 'MAX', max_results, 'WITHSCORES', 'WITHPAYLOADS'
            )
            
            for i in range(0, len(company_suggestions), 3):
                if i + 2 < len(company_suggestions):
                    text = company_suggestions[i]
                    score = float(company_suggestions[i + 1])
                    payload = json.loads(company_suggestions[i + 2]) if company_suggestions[i + 2] else {}
                    
                    # Company-specific contextual scoring
                    contextual_score = score
                    if payload.get('hiring_status') == 'active':
                        contextual_score += 25
                    if payload.get('tier') == 'premium':
                        contextual_score += 30
                        
                    all_suggestions.append({
                        'text': text,
                        'category': 'company',
                        'score': round(contextual_score, 1),
                        'hiring_status': payload.get('hiring_status', 'unknown'),
                        'company_size': payload.get('company_size', 'unknown'),
                        'active_jobs': payload.get('active_jobs', 0),
                        'tier': payload.get('tier', 'standard'),
                        'icon': '🏢' if payload.get('tier') != 'premium' else '⭐'
                    })
        
        # Sort by contextual score and limit results
        all_suggestions.sort(key=lambda x: x['score'], reverse=True)
        final_suggestions = all_suggestions[:max_results]
        
        return JsonResponse({
            'query': query,
            'suggestions': final_suggestions,
            'count': len(final_suggestions),
            'context': user_context,
            'categories_found': list(set(s['category'] for s in final_suggestions)),
            'max_score': max([s['score'] for s in final_suggestions]) if final_suggestions else 0
        })
        
    except Exception as e:
        return JsonResponse({'error': str(e), 'query': query}, status=500)
Printout:

FT.SUGDEL - Delete Suggestion from Dictionary

Purpose: Removes a suggestion string from an auto-complete dictionary.
Syntax: FT.SUGDEL key string
Parameters:
  • key - Auto-complete dictionary name
  • string - Suggestion text to remove

Return: 1 if the suggestion was found and deleted, 0 otherwise
Django Example: Auto-Complete Maintenance Service 
# services/autocomplete_maintenance.py
import redis
from django.core.management.base import BaseCommand
from django.utils import timezone
from .models import JobPost, Author

redis_client = redis.Redis(host='localhost', port=6379, decode_responses=True)

class AutocompleteMaintenanceService:
    @staticmethod
    def cleanup_outdated_suggestions():
        """Clean up outdated and inappropriate suggestions"""
        
        print("🧹 Starting auto-complete cleanup...")
        
        # Remove outdated job titles
        outdated_job_titles = [
            'Webmaster', 'Flash Developer', 'Internet Explorer Developer',
            'ColdFusion Developer', 'Perl Programmer', 'FTP Administrator',
            'HTML Coder', 'Table-based Web Designer'
        ]
        
        job_removed = 0
        for title in outdated_job_titles:
            result = redis_client.execute_command('FT.SUGDEL', 'job_titles:suggestions', title)
            if result == 1:
                job_removed += 1
                print(f"❌ Removed outdated job title: {title}")
            
        print(f"✅ Removed {job_removed} outdated job titles")
        
        # Remove inactive companies (no jobs in last 6 months)
        cutoff_date = timezone.now() - timezone.timedelta(days=180)
        inactive_companies = Author.objects.filter(
            jobpost__date__lt=cutoff_date
        ).distinct().values_list('company', flat=True)
        
        company_removed = 0
        for company in inactive_companies:
            result = redis_client.execute_command('FT.SUGDEL', 'companies:suggestions', company)
            if result == 1:
                company_removed += 1
                print(f"❌ Removed inactive company: {company}")
                
        print(f"✅ Removed {company_removed} inactive companies")
        
        # Remove test/spam entries
        spam_patterns = [
            'test', 'testing123', 'asdf', 'qwerty', 'sample', 'demo',
            'placeholder', 'temp', 'fake', 'spam', '12345'
        ]
        
        spam_removed = 0
        dictionaries = ['job_titles:suggestions', 'companies:suggestions']
        
        for dict_name in dictionaries:
            for pattern in spam_patterns:
                result = redis_client.execute_command('FT.SUGDEL', dict_name, pattern)
                if result == 1:
                    spam_removed += 1
                    print(f"🚫 Removed spam entry: {pattern} from {dict_name}")
        
        print(f"✅ Removed {spam_removed} spam entries")
        
        return {
            'job_titles_removed': job_removed,
            'companies_removed': company_removed,
            'spam_removed': spam_removed,
            'total_removed': job_removed + company_removed + spam_removed
        }
    
    @staticmethod
    def update_suggestion_priority():
        """Update suggestion priorities based on current activity"""
        
        print("📊 Updating suggestion priorities...")
        
        # Get current job posting activity
        recent_jobs = JobPost.objects.filter(
            date__gte=timezone.now() - timezone.timedelta(days=30)
        ).values_list('title', flat=True)
        
        recent_counts = {}
        for title in recent_jobs:
            recent_counts[title] = recent_counts.get(title, 0) + 1
        
        updated = 0
        for title, recent_activity in recent_counts.items():
            # Remove old entry
            redis_client.execute_command('FT.SUGDEL', 'job_titles:suggestions', title)
            
            # Re-add with boosted score based on recent activity
            new_score = recent_activity * 20 + 50  # Base score + activity bonus
            
            redis_client.execute_command(
                'FT.SUGADD', 'job_titles:suggestions', title, new_score,
                'PAYLOAD', f'{{"recent_activity": {recent_activity}, "last_updated": "{timezone.now().isoformat()}", "trending": true}}'
            )
            
            updated += 1
            print(f"🔄 Updated {title}: recent activity {recent_activity}, new score {new_score}")
        
        print(f"✅ Updated priorities for {updated} job titles")
        return updated

# Management command
class Command(BaseCommand):
    help = 'Maintain auto-complete suggestion dictionaries'
    
    def add_arguments(self, parser):
        parser.add_argument('--action', choices=['cleanup', 'update_priorities', 'stats'], 
                          default='cleanup', help='Maintenance action')
    
    def handle(self, *args, **options):
        action = options['action']
        
        if action == 'cleanup':
            results = AutocompleteMaintenanceService.cleanup_outdated_suggestions()
            self.stdout.write(f"🎯 Cleanup complete: {results['total_removed']} entries removed")
            
        elif action == 'update_priorities':
            updated = AutocompleteMaintenanceService.update_suggestion_priority()
            self.stdout.write(f"📈 Updated priorities for {updated} suggestions")
            
        elif action == 'stats':
            job_count = redis_client.execute_command('FT.SUGLEN', 'job_titles:suggestions')
            company_count = redis_client.execute_command('FT.SUGLEN', 'companies:suggestions')
            
            self.stdout.write(f"📊 Auto-complete Statistics:")
            self.stdout.write(f"   Job titles: {job_count}")
            self.stdout.write(f"   Companies: {company_count}")
            self.stdout.write(f"   Total: {job_count + company_count}")
Printout:

FT.SUGLEN - Get Suggestion Dictionary Size

Purpose: Returns the number of suggestions in an auto-complete dictionary.
Syntax: FT.SUGLEN key
Parameters:
  • key - Auto-complete dictionary name

Return: Number of suggestions in the dictionary
Django Example: Auto-Complete Analytics Dashboard 
# views.py - Auto-complete analytics and monitoring
import redis
from django.shortcuts import render
from django.http import JsonResponse
from django.contrib.admin.views.decorators import staff_member_required
from django.utils import timezone

redis_client = redis.Redis(host='localhost', port=6379, decode_responses=True)

@staff_member_required
def autocomplete_dashboard(request):
    """Admin dashboard for auto-complete analytics"""
    
    # Get dictionary statistics
    dictionaries = [
        ('job_titles:suggestions', 'Job Titles'),
        ('companies:suggestions', 'Companies'),
        ('skills:suggestions', 'Skills'),
        ('locations:suggestions', 'Locations')
    ]
    
    stats = {}
    total_suggestions = 0
    
    for dict_key, display_name in dictionaries:
        try:
            size = redis_client.execute_command('FT.SUGLEN', dict_key)
            stats[dict_key] = {
                'name': display_name,
                'size': size,
                'status': 'healthy' if size > 0 else 'empty',
                'health_score': min(100, (size / 50) * 100) if size > 0 else 0
            }
            total_suggestions += size
            
        except Exception as e:
            stats[dict_key] = {
                'name': display_name,
                'size': 0,
                'status': 'error',
                'error': str(e),
                'health_score': 0
            }
    
    # Calculate system health
    healthy_dicts = sum(1 for s in stats.values() if s['status'] == 'healthy')
    system_health = (healthy_dicts / len(dictionaries)) * 100
    
    # Get sample suggestions for preview
    samples = {}
    for dict_key, display_name in dictionaries:
        if stats[dict_key]['size'] > 0:
            try:
                # Get sample suggestions with common prefixes
                sample_suggestions = []
                for prefix in ['a', 'b', 'c', 'p']:  # Try common starting letters
                    suggestions = redis_client.execute_command(
                        'FT.SUGGET', dict_key, prefix, 'MAX', 3
                    )
                    sample_suggestions.extend(suggestions)
                    if len(sample_suggestions) >= 5:
                        break
                
                samples[dict_key] = sample_suggestions[:5]
            except:
                samples[dict_key] = []
    
    dashboard_data = {
        'timestamp': timezone.now().isoformat(),
        'dictionaries': stats,
        'total_suggestions': total_suggestions,
        'system_health': round(system_health, 1),
        'healthy_dictionaries': healthy_dicts,
        'total_dictionaries': len(dictionaries),
        'sample_suggestions': samples,
        'recommendations': generate_maintenance_recommendations(stats)
    }
    
    if request.headers.get('Accept') == 'application/json':
        return JsonResponse(dashboard_data)
    
    return render(request, 'admin/autocomplete_dashboard.html', {
        'dashboard_data': dashboard_data
    })

def generate_maintenance_recommendations(stats):
    """Generate maintenance recommendations"""
    recommendations = []
    
    for dict_key, data in stats.items():
        if data['status'] == 'empty':
            recommendations.append({
                'type': 'warning',
                'message': f"{data['name']} dictionary is empty",
                'action': f"Build initial suggestions for {data['name'].lower()}"
            })
        elif data['size'] > 1000:
            recommendations.append({
                'type': 'info', 
                'message': f"{data['name']} dictionary is large ({data['size']} entries)",
                'action': f"Consider cleaning up outdated {data['name'].lower()} suggestions"
            })
    
    return recommendations

# API endpoint for real-time monitoring
@csrf_exempt
def autocomplete_stats_api(request):
    """Real-time auto-complete statistics API"""
    
    dictionaries = ['job_titles:suggestions', 'companies:suggestions', 'skills:suggestions']
    
    stats = {}
    for dict_name in dictionaries:
        try:
            size = redis_client.execute_command('FT.SUGLEN', dict_name)
            stats[dict_name.split(':')[0]] = {
                'count': size,
                'status': 'active' if size > 0 else 'empty',
                'last_checked': timezone.now().isoformat()
            }
        except Exception as e:
            stats[dict_name.split(':')[0]] = {
                'count': 0,
                'status': 'error',
                'error': str(e)
            }
    
    return JsonResponse({
        'dictionaries': stats,
        'total': sum(s['count'] for s in stats.values() if isinstance(s.get('count'), int)),
        'timestamp': timezone.now().isoformat(),
        'system_status': 'healthy' if all(s['count'] > 0 for s in stats.values()) else 'needs_attention'
    })

💡 Implementation Note: The Auto-suggest commands provide a complete solution for intelligent autocomplete functionality in Django applications. Combined with proper maintenance, contextual scoring, and analytics monitoring, these commands enable sophisticated search experiences with real-time suggestions, fuzzy matching, and personalized recommendations.

📊 T-digest Commands

T-digest sketches provide efficient percentile and quantile estimations for large datasets. Perfect for Django analytics, performance monitoring, and statistical analysis without storing all data points.

TDIGEST.CREATE - Create T-digest Sketch

Purpose: Creates a new t-digest sketch for percentile estimation.
Syntax: TDIGEST.CREATE key [COMPRESSION compression]
Return: OK if successful
Example 1: Track salary percentiles 
import redis
r = redis.Redis(decode_responses=True)

# Create t-digest for salary analysis
r.execute_command('TDIGEST.CREATE', 'salary_stats')
print("Salary tracker created")
Salary tracker created
Example 2: Response time monitoring 
# Create t-digest for API response times
r.execute_command('TDIGEST.CREATE', 'api_response_times', 'COMPRESSION', 400)
print("Response time tracker ready")
Response time tracker ready

TDIGEST.ADD - Add Observations

Purpose: Adds observations to a t-digest sketch.
Syntax: TDIGEST.ADD key value [value ...]
Return: OK if successful
Example 1: Add job salaries 
# Add salary data points
r.execute_command('TDIGEST.ADD', 'salary_stats', 75000, 82000, 95000, 68000)
print("Salaries added")
Salaries added
Example 2: Track response times 
# Add API response times (ms)
r.execute_command('TDIGEST.ADD', 'api_response_times', 45.2, 123.8, 67.1)
print("Response times recorded")
Response times recorded

TDIGEST.QUANTILE - Get Quantiles

Purpose: Returns quantile estimates for given fractions.
Syntax: TDIGEST.QUANTILE key quantile [quantile ...]
Return: Array of quantile values
Example 1: Salary percentiles 
# Get 50th, 75th, 95th percentiles
result = r.execute_command('TDIGEST.QUANTILE', 'salary_stats', 0.5, 0.75, 0.95)
print(f"Percentiles: 50th=${result[0]:.0f}, 75th=${result[1]:.0f}, 95th=${result[2]:.0f}")
Percentiles: 50th=$78500, 75th=$88500, 95th=$95000
Example 2: Response time SLAs 
# Check p95 and p99 response times
sla_percentiles = r.execute_command('TDIGEST.QUANTILE', 'api_response_times', 0.95, 0.99)
print(f"p95: {sla_percentiles[0]:.1f}ms, p99: {sla_percentiles[1]:.1f}ms")
p95: 120.2ms, p99: 123.8ms

TDIGEST.CDF - Cumulative Distribution

Purpose: Returns fraction of observations below given values.
Syntax: TDIGEST.CDF key value [value ...]
Return: Array of CDF fractions
Example 1: Salary distribution 
# What % earn less than $80k?
cdf = r.execute_command('TDIGEST.CDF', 'salary_stats', 80000)
print(f"{cdf[0]*100:.1f}% earn less than $80,000")
62.5% earn less than $80,000
Example 2: Performance benchmarks 
# What % of requests under 100ms?
fast_requests = r.execute_command('TDIGEST.CDF', 'api_response_times', 100)
print(f"{fast_requests[0]*100:.1f}% requests under 100ms")
66.7% requests under 100ms

TDIGEST.RANK - Get Ranks

Purpose: Returns estimated ranks for given values.
Syntax: TDIGEST.RANK key value [value ...]
Return: Array of rank estimates
Example 1: Salary ranking 
# Rank of $85k salary
rank = r.execute_command('TDIGEST.RANK', 'salary_stats', 85000)
print(f"$85k ranks at position {rank[0]:.1f}")
$85k ranks at position 2.5
Example 2: Performance ranking 
# Rank 90ms response time
perf_rank = r.execute_command('TDIGEST.RANK', 'api_response_times', 90.0)
print(f"90ms ranks at {perf_rank[0]:.1f}")
90ms ranks at 2.0

TDIGEST.BYRANK - Value by Rank

Purpose: Returns values for given ranks.
Syntax: TDIGEST.BYRANK key rank [rank ...]
Return: Array of estimated values
Example 1: Top salary by rank 
# Get top 2 salaries
top_salaries = r.execute_command('TDIGEST.BYRANK', 'salary_stats', 3, 2)
print(f"2nd highest: ${top_salaries[1]:.0f}, 3rd: ${top_salaries[0]:.0f}")
2nd highest: $95000, 3rd: $82000
Example 2: Slowest responses 
# Get slowest response time
slowest = r.execute_command('TDIGEST.BYRANK', 'api_response_times', 3)
print(f"Slowest: {slowest[0]:.1f}ms")
Slowest: 123.8ms

TDIGEST.MIN / TDIGEST.MAX - Min/Max Values

Purpose: Returns minimum or maximum observed values.
Syntax: TDIGEST.MIN key or TDIGEST.MAX key
Return: Minimum or maximum value
Example 1: Salary range 
# Get salary range
min_sal = r.execute_command('TDIGEST.MIN', 'salary_stats')
max_sal = r.execute_command('TDIGEST.MAX', 'salary_stats')
print(f"Salary range: ${min_sal} - ${max_sal}")
Salary range: $68000.0 - $95000.0
Example 2: Response time bounds 
# Get fastest/slowest response
fastest = r.execute_command('TDIGEST.MIN', 'api_response_times')
slowest = r.execute_command('TDIGEST.MAX', 'api_response_times')
print(f"Response range: {fastest}ms - {slowest}ms")
Response range: 45.2ms - 123.8ms

TDIGEST.INFO - Sketch Information

Purpose: Returns information about the t-digest sketch.
Syntax: TDIGEST.INFO key
Return: Array with sketch statistics
Example 1: Salary stats info 
# Get sketch details
info = r.execute_command('TDIGEST.INFO', 'salary_stats')
print(f"Observations: {info[3]}, Compression: {info[1]}")
Observations: 4, Compression: 100
Example 2: Monitor sketch size 
# Check memory usage
info = r.execute_command('TDIGEST.INFO', 'api_response_times')
print(f"Memory: {info[5]} bytes, Count: {info[3]}")
Memory: 58 bytes, Count: 3

TDIGEST.RESET - Reset Sketch

Purpose: Resets a t-digest sketch to empty state.
Syntax: TDIGEST.RESET key
Return: OK if successful
Example 1: Reset salary data 
# Clear all salary data
r.execute_command('TDIGEST.RESET', 'salary_stats')
print("Salary data cleared")
Salary data cleared
Example 2: Daily metrics reset 
# Reset for new day
r.execute_command('TDIGEST.RESET', 'api_response_times')
print("Daily metrics reset")
Daily metrics reset

TDIGEST.MERGE - Merge Sketches

Purpose: Merges multiple t-digest sketches into one.
Syntax: TDIGEST.MERGE destkey sourcekey [sourcekey ...]
Return: OK if successful
Example 1: Combine team salaries 
# Merge department salaries
r.execute_command('TDIGEST.MERGE', 'all_salaries', 'dev_salaries', 'qa_salaries')
print("Salary data merged")
Salary data merged
Example 2: Aggregate server metrics 
# Combine server response times
r.execute_command('TDIGEST.MERGE', 'total_response', 'server1_times', 'server2_times')
print("Server metrics combined")
Server metrics combined
